The paper proposes a privacy-preserving data mining framework using mixture models, with contributions from authors like Yu Zhu, Lei Liu, Chris Clifton, and others, focusing on balancing performance, mutual information loss, and privacy metrics.
The paper proposes a reinforcement learning-based Markov Decision Process framework for cross-channel marketing optimization, validated by authors including C. Apte, Vince P. Thomas, and others, showing a 7-8% profit increase in real-world tests with Saks Fifth Avenue.
The paper presents an interactive system using decision tree classifiers for land cover modeling and remote sensing image mining, integrating spectral, DEM, and GIS data, with contributions from authors Giovanni Marchisio, Krzysztof Koperski, Carsten Tusk, and Selim Aksoy.
The paper, co-authored by Jon Kleinberg, Lars Backstrom, Amin Saberi, Xiangyang Lan, Daniel Huttenlocher, Jennifer Chayes, Mohammad Mahdian, and Christian Borgs, proposes using cross-post networks to analyze Usenet newsgroups' community structure, revealing small-world properties and presenting a spectral clustering algorithm for topical classification.
The paper discusses efficient feature selection methods for high-dimensional scientific datasets, with contributions from authors Chandrika Kamath, Shawn Newsam, and Erick Cantu-Paz, covering challenges and strategies in astronomy, plasma physics, and remote sensing.
The paper proposes a general ensemble method incorporating data quality matrices to improve predictive accuracy, with contributions from authors Ian Davidson, Giri K. Tayi, Ashwin Satyanarayana, and Ashish Grover.
The paper presents an automated two-step system for mapping supplier part numbers in BOMs to internal part numbers, involving authors Moninder Singh, Jayant Kalagnanam, Yuk Wah Wong, Sudhir Verma, and Michael Patek, to replace manual processes and improve efficiency.
The paper proposes a real-time topic trend analysis framework using a dynamically learned finite mixture model, with contributions from authors like Satoshi Morinaga, Rene Schult, and others, focusing on topic structures, emerging topics, and characterization, demonstrated with help desk data.
The paper, authored by Takayuki Nakata and Jun-ichi Takeuchi, proposes a travel time prediction method using probe-car data with AR models, seasonal adjustment, state space models, and MDL criterion, validated on Nagoya data.
The paper demonstrates efficient SQL implementation of K-means clustering with optimizations, co-authored by Zhang, Ramakrishnan, Ordonez, Livny, Aggarwal, and Yu.
The paper justifies and evaluates heuristic document preprocessing techniques like IDF, normalization, and log transformations to improve naive Bayes classification and multinomial mixture clustering for text categorization and clustering tasks, with contributions from authors Byron Dom, Dmitry Pavlov, Ramnath Balasubramanyan, Shyam Kapur, Jignashu Parikh, and Aleksander Kolcz.
The paper explores the use of random forests and support vector machines for classifying individuals into three disease and treatment groups based on metabolomic data, addressing challenges like non-normality, missing data, and high correlations while linking selected predictors to disease biochemistry, with contributions from authors Young Truong, Xiaodong Lin, and Chris Beecher.
The paper introduces Analytical View (AV) in MBF for OLTP-OLAP integration, authored by Adam Yeh, Youxuan Jin, Jonathan Tang, and Sam Skrivan, featuring automated model transformation, BI Entities, and IntelliDrill to eliminate ETL complexity.
